            data-share-method="comments"
            data-uotrack="InlineShareCommentsBtn"><span class="inline-share-count inline-share-count-comments">

            </span><span class="inline-share-btn-label inline-share-btn-label-comments">COMMENT</span></span><span
        class="inline-share-btn inline-share-btn-email"
        data-share-method="email"
        data-uotrack="InlineShareEmailBtn"><span class="inline-share-count inline-share-count-email"></span><span class="inline-share-btn-label inline-share-btn-label-email">EMAIL</span></span><span
         class="inline-share-btn inline-share-btn-more"
         data-share-method="facebook"
         data-uotrack="InlineShareMoreBtn"><span class="inline-share-count inline-share-count-more"></span><span class="inline-share-btn-label inline-share-btn-label-more">MORE</span></span></div></div><p>HOUSTON — Finally, officially, completely and certainly, Deflategate is over.</p><p>It ended Sunday night at 9:30 local time at NRG Stadium, when New England running back James White scored his third touchdown, a 2-yard run four minutes into overtime, to end Super Bowl LI with a 34-28 Patriots’ victory.</p><p>It ended when Tom Brady, the man who served a four-game suspension at the start of this season for tampering with the air pressure in his footballs more than two years ago, won his fifth Super Bowl, the most of any quarterback in history.</p><p>It ended with the sterling performance that earned Brady his unprecedented fourth Super Bowl MVP award. It was over when the Patriots completed an historic comeback from a 25-point deficit. It ended with that clutch Super Bowl-winning drive, just another in Brady's collection of clutch Super Bowl winning drives.</p><p><strong>MORE SUPER BOWL:</strong></p><div id="module-position-PwKk8mrOZh0" class="story-asset oembed-asset"><div class="story-oembed-wrap "><div 
        class="js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-usa-today story-oembed-type-link"
        data-oembed-type="link"
        data-oembed-provider="usa-today"><style>
    .oembed-asset-link { border-bottom: 1px solid #e1e1e1; }
    .oembed-link-anchor { display: block; clear: both; }
    p.oembed-link-desc { font-size: 100%; color: #666; font-weight: normal; margin: 0 14px 14px 14px; font-family: 'Futura Today Light'; text-align: left; line-height: 120%; }
</style><div class="oembed-asset oembed-asset-link oembed-asset-usa-today oembed-simple-link-container"><a href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/sports/nfl/patriots/2017/02/05/robert-kraft-roger-goodell-deflategate-tom-brady-new-england/97537406/" data-track-label="newrecircinline" class="oembed-simple-link oembed-link-anchor"><p class="oembed-link-desc">Robert Kraft takes shot at Roger Goodell after &#39;sweetest&#39; Super Bowl win</p><div style="clear: both;"></div></a></div></div></div></div><div id="module-position-PwKk8mr0z38" class="story-asset oembed-asset"><div class="story-oembed-wrap "><div 
        class="js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-usa-today story-oembed-type-link"
        data-oembed-type="link"
        data-oembed-provider="usa-today"><style>
    .oembed-asset-link { border-bottom: 1px solid #e1e1e1; }
    .oembed-link-anchor { display: block; clear: both; }
    p.oembed-link-desc { font-size: 100%; color: #666; font-weight: normal; margin: 0 14px 14px 14px; font-family: 'Futura Today Light'; text-align: left; line-height: 120%; }
</style><div class="oembed-asset oembed-asset-link oembed-asset-usa-today oembed-simple-link-container"><a href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/sports/nfl/patriots/2017/02/05/tom-brady-super-bowl-2017-new-england-patriots/97530620/" data-track-label="newrecircinline" class="oembed-simple-link oembed-link-anchor"><p class="oembed-link-desc">Tom Brady stands alone as NFL&#39;s greatest after rescuing Patriots in Super Bowl</p><div style="clear: both;"></div></a></div></div></div></div><div id="module-position-PwKk8mqhZsU" class="story-asset oembed-asset"><div class="story-oembed-wrap "><div 
        class="js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-usa-today story-oembed-type-link"
        data-oembed-type="link"
        data-oembed-provider="usa-today"><style>
    .oembed-asset-link { border-bottom: 1px solid #e1e1e1; }
    .oembed-link-anchor { display: block; clear: both; }
    p.oembed-link-desc { font-size: 100%; color: #666; font-weight: normal; margin: 0 14px 14px 14px; font-family: 'Futura Today Light'; text-align: left; line-height: 120%; }
</style><div class="oembed-asset oembed-asset-link oembed-asset-usa-today oembed-simple-link-container"><a href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/sports/columnist/nancy-armour/2017/02/06/julian-edelman-catch-super-bowl-51-new-england-patriots-atlanta-falcons/97539526/" data-track-label="newrecircinline" class="oembed-simple-link oembed-link-anchor"><p class="oembed-link-desc">Patriots deserved Julian Edelman&#39;s spectacular catch</p><div style="clear: both;"></div></a></div></div></div></div><p>You want to bring up Deflategate now? Go ahead and try, but you’re on your own. The NFL has been checking the pressure in its footballs more carefully the past two years, and all Brady has done is win two of the last three Super Bowls.</p><p>“Two years ago, we won our fourth Super Bowl down in Arizona and I told our fans that was the sweetest one of all,” Patriots owner Robert Kraft said to the crowd after the game. “But a lot has transpired during the last two years, and I don’t think that needs any explanation.”</p><p>I don’t either. NFL Commissioner Roger Goodell was booed loudly by Patriots fans for the entirety of his statement to Kraft as he handed him the Lombardi Trophy, proving Deflategate might be over, but it certainly has not been forgotten in Boston.</p><p>Actually, it’s time for New England fans to let it go. You won. Declare victory. Move on.</p><p>Whether you think Brady was a cheater, or you’re still angry that he was viewed (and punished) as the culprit, Deflategate is a footnote now. It just doesn’t stand a chance against the totality of Brady’s scintillating record.</p><p>Consider this: the 39-year-old has now completed 207 out of 309 passes for 2,071 yards and 15 touchdowns with five interceptions in all of his Super Bowl appearances. No other quarterback in history has more than 1,200 yards passing in Super Bowl play, and Brady’s 207 completions are more than twice as many as any other quarterback in Super Bowl history.</p><p>Tom Brady is the greatest quarterback in NFL history, Deflategate or no Deflategate.</p><p>“You just saw that for yourself,” said New England safety Patrick Chung. “He brought us down and he brought us another Super Bowl, so whoever says that he is not the greatest, you guys are stupid.”</p><p>We are not stupid.</p><p>“He is the Michael Jordan of football,” said Patriots safety Duron Harmon. “The greatest of all-time is Tom Brady.”</p><p>Other people who don’t play on his team agreed.</p><p>A sampling from Twitter:</p><p>Justin Timberlake: “Tom. Brady. G.O.A.T.”</p><p>Kobe Bryant: “5 rings can’t be deflated.”</p><div id="module-position-PwKk8mrqae0" class="story-asset oembed-asset"><div class="story-oembed-wrap "><div 
        class="js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-twitter story-oembed-type-rich"
        data-oembed-type="rich"
        data-oembed-provider="twitter"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet"><p lang="en" dir="ltr">5 rings can&#39;t be deflated <a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/Brady?src=hash">#Brady</a><a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/Muse?src=hash">#Muse</a></p>&mdash; Kobe Bryant (@kobebryant) <a href="https://twitter.com/kobebryant/status/828447492358279168">February 6, 2017</a></blockquote></div></div></div><p>LeBron James: “Brady=GOAT. CONGRATS brother!!”</p><p>Tom Glavine: Congrats to my Pats…great season Falcons…suck it Goodell.”</p><p>See what I mean about it being time for New Englanders to let it go?</p><p>Brady has. He was asked a couple of times after the game about the “struggles” the franchise has endured. He wasn’t biting.</p><p>“There was a lot at stake tonight,” he said. “You know, we played our tails off all season to get to this point and it’s hard to win a game in the NFL. And to beat this team and to get down, 28-3, it was just a lot of mental toughness by our team and we’re all going to remember this for the rest of our lives.”</p><p>A reporter tried one more time.</p><p>“We’ve done pretty good over the last few years, you know?” Brady said. “We were in the AFC Championship last year and won the Super Bowl two years ago, so I don’t think anyone’s feeling bad for the Patriots.”</p><p>And just like that, the last embers of Deflategate went dark.</p><div id="module-position-PwKk8mqX_0Y" class="story-asset gallery-asset"><div class="card-film inactive"></div><div class="sidebar-gallery-btn active"></div><div class="companion-story-gallery"><div class="gallery-sidebar-panel"><span class="gallery-sidebar-close"></span><div class="gallery-sidebar-toolbox share-pane social-pane "><span class="util-bar-flyout-nav-btn-wrap"><span
